## 2                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

## KEAM – 2026
## INFORMATION AT A GLANCE
-     Online Application submission : From 05.01.2026 (Monday)
-    Last date for submission of Online Application
including Fee payment  : 31.01.2026, 05:00 PM (Saturday)
-   Last date for Online submission of supporting
documents :  07.02.2026 (Saturday)
## 4.   Downloading Online Admit Cards :  01.04.2026 Onwards
-   Dates of Engineering Entrance Examination :   13.04.2026 to 25.04.2026

-      Venue of Examination :  As indicated in the Admit Card
-   Time schedule for the Examination (IST)
(a) Reporting to the Examination Center :  12:00 PM
(b) Entry to the Examination Hall :  01:30 PM
(c) Mock Test :  01:45 PM
(d) Last entry to the Examination Hall :  01:50 PM
(e) Examination starts :  02:00 PM
(f) End of Examination :  05:00 PM
-      Materials permitted in the examination hall       :  Admit Card, Photo ID proof  as per the
admit Card, Transparent Ball-Point pen

-       Rough work :  Papers for rough work will be provided
in the examination hall

-    Declaration of Results:
Result of Engineering/Pharmacy Entrance
Examination                                                           :  On or before 10-05-2026

Rank lists of Engineering, B.Pharm Courses     :  On or before 20-06-2026

## 3                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM


## IMPORTANT INFORMATION



- Candidates  applying  for  admission  to  any  of  the  following  courses - Engineering,
Architecture, B.Pharm, MBBS, BDS, Ayurveda, Homoeopathy, Siddha, Unani, Agriculture,
B.Sc.(Hons) Co-operation & Banking/ B.Sc (Hons) Agri  Business Management, Climate
Change  &  Environmental  Science,  B.Tech  Biotechnology  (under  KAU),  Forestry,
Veterinary and Fisheries - should apply online on or before the last date.
- Application and supporting documents submission is possible ONLY in online mode through the
website – www.cee.kerala.gov.in of Commissioner for Entrance Examinations, Kerala.
- Application  Acknowledgement  Page  of  the  online  application  must  be  retained  for  future
reference. Do not  send the printout of the Application Acknowledgement Page or other
documents to the office of the Commissioner for Entrance Examinations (CEE).
- Applicant  should  ensure  the  following  before  submission  of  online application  and  uploading
supporting documents:
i. All the required certificates are properly filled in and signed by the competent authority and
affixed office seal at the specified places before uploading to the online application.
ii. The  photograph  and  image  of  signature  uploaded  must  be  clear  and  conforming  to  the
prescribed specifications.
iii. The applicant should select the course/courses which he/she desires to study while applying
online.
iv. The  candidate  should  maintain  confidentiality  of  the  password  created  at  the  time  of
registration for submission of online application and keep it in safe custody till the end of
the allotment process.
The defects in the Online Application will be displayed in the Candidate Portal of the website
of  CEE. The candidate should visit the website of the CEE regularly for notifications and
updates.    The  defects,  if  any,  which  will  be  made  available  in  the  Candidate  Portal,  should  be
cleared by the candidates within the stipulated time notified by the CEE.  No memo will be sent by
post from this office on matters with regard to Application, Allotment, and Admission etc.
Defect  memo  will  be  issued  through  the  ‘Candidate  Portal’ only  and  the  information
regarding the same will be intimated via e-mail/ SMS/Sandes app.
- Candidates should submit only one online application for admission to any or all of the
courses in KEAM 2026.
-  Candidates except SC/ST/OEC category should upload income certificate while applying online
for availing income based fee concession/scholarship.
-  Online  option  confirmation  is  mandatory  for  participating  in  each  phase  of  allotment,  unless
otherwise notified.

െг˔്  1: രജിേІഷൻ:-അേപűകͭെട  േപര്,  ജനന  തീയതി,  ഇ-െമയിൽ  ഐ.ഡി,

ňറിƿ വ͒ക.

## Ŋതńമായി നൽേകȗതാണ്. എǥിനീയറിംഗ്, ആർōിെടക്ചർ,  ബി.ഫാം, െമഡിōൽ/
െമഡിōൽ അʓബʫ േകാѯകൾ എʱിവെയΗാം ഒͭ അേപűയിൽ തെʱ

സംവരണം, ഭിʱേശഷിōാർŎы  സംവരണം, വńവБ  5.2  ൽ െകാdzȳിǸы  ̨േതńക

Бാനȳ് േരഖെ˔dzȳിയിരിōണം. നൽകിയ വിവരƹെളΗാം ŊതńΚം ˆർȩΚമാെണʱ്
േബാധńെ˔Ƿാൽ അʗിമ സമർ˔ണം (Final submission) നടȳാΚʱതാണ്.
## െг˔്  3: അേപűാ  ഫീസ് ഒdzōൽ:-നിർɮിϓ അേപű  ഫീസ്  ഓൺൈലനായി

## 6                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

a) സാ̲ദായിക  സംവരണം ആവശń̲ыവർ  ഓൺൈലനായി  അപ്േലാഡ്  െചേͪȗ
## േരഖകൾ
i.  സാ̳ഹികΚം, വിദńാഭńാസപരΚമായി പിʱാōം നിൽŎʱ  (SEBC) വിഭാഗōാർ
േകരള സർōാരിെ˂ പഠനാവശńƹൾōായി നൽňʱ നിΩിത മാȱകയിͰы
േനാൺūീമിെലയർ സർǷിഫിōѳ് വിേΗജ് ഓഫീസറിൽ നിʲം വാƹി അപ്േലാഡ്
െചേͪȗതാണ്. േകʨ സർōാർ ആവശńƹൾŎыേതാ  േജാലി സംബʫമായ
ആവശńƹൾŎыേതാ  ആയ സർǷിഫിōѳ്  സŇീകാരńമΗ. (സർǷിഫിōѳിെ˂
മാȱക്͑ അʓബʫം XXVII കാȕക).

ii.  SC/ST വിഭാഗōാർ ജാതി സർǷിഫിōѳ് ബʫെ˔Ƿ തഹസിൽദാരിൽ നിʲം വാƹി
അപ്േലാഡ്  െചേͪȗതാണ്.    Screening  committee  Pg.40 (സർǷിഫിōѳിെ˂
മാȱക്͑ അʓബʫം XXIX കാȕക)

iii.   ഒഇസി   വിഭാഗȳിൽെ˔Ƿ   (OEC) അേപűകർ   േകരള സർōാരിെ˂
പഠനാവശńƹൾōായി നൽňʱ േനാൺūീമിെലയർ സർǷിഫിōѳ്  വിേΗജ്
ഓഫീസറിൽ നിʲം വാƹി  അപ്േലാഡ്  െചേͪȗതാണ്. (സർǷിഫിōѳിെ˂
മാȱക്͑ അʓബʫം XXVII കാȕക)
iv.  േനാൺūീമിെലയർ വിഭാഗȳിൽ ഉൾെ˔ടാȳ    OEC അേപűകർ

സർǷിഫിōѳ്   അപ്േലാഡ്   െചേͪȗതാണ്.   (സർǷിഫിōѳിെ˂ മാȱക്͑
അʓബʫം  XXXIII കാȕക). അേപűകെ˂  എസ്.എസ്.എൽ.സി/ വിദńാഭńാസ
േരഖയിൽ ജാതി/ സ̲ദായം Ŋതńമായി േരഖെ˔dzȳിയിǸെȗƵിൽ ആയത് വിേΗജ്
ഓഫീസർ നൽňʱ സ̲ദായ സർǷിഫിōѳിʓ പകരമായി പരിഗണിŎʱതാണ്.

v.   േ ̨ാെИŔസ് അʓബʫം  X(a)  ൽ ഉൾെ˔dzȳിയിǸы സ̲ദായȳിൽെ˔Ƿ

വͭമാന സർǷിഫിōѴം ബʫെ˔Ƿ വിേΗജ് ഓഫീസറിൽ നിʲം വാƹി അപ്േലാഡ്
െചേͪȗതാണ്.  (സർǷിഫിōѳിെ˂ മാȱക്͑ അʓബʫം  XXXI,  XXXIII കാȕക).

## 11                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

## 1.        INTRODUCTION
1.1 Prospectus  for  Admission  to  Professional  Degree  Courses  2026,  which  has  been
approved  by  the  Government  of  Kerala,  is  published  herewith.  It  contains  general
information and rules relating to the Entrance Examinations and allotment process for
Admission  to  Professional  Degree  Courses  2026  and  other  connected  matters.
Candidates are required to go through the Prospectus carefully and acquaint themselves
with all the relevant information relating to the examinations/allotments. Candidates
are  also  required  to  visit  the  website  of  the  Commissioner  for  Entrance
Examinations   ‘www.cee.kerala.gov.in’   regularly   for   notifications   and
announcements.
No memo will be sent by post from this office on matters with regard to Application,
Allotment,  and  Admission  etc.  Defect  memo  will  be  issued  through  the  ‘Candidate
Portal’only   and   information   regarding   the   same   will   be   intimated   via
email/SMS/Sandes app.
1.2   (a) The Prospectus issued in previous years is not valid for the year 2026.
(b) The English version of the Prospectus shall only be considered as authentic, in the
case of dispute in any of the Clauses of the Prospectus for admission to Professional
Degree Courses, 2026 (KEAM-2026).
1.3   This Prospectus sets out the rules and regulations for selection and admission to the
following professional degree courses conducted by the various authorities within the
State of Kerala.
## 1.3.1 Engineering Courses:
Bachelor of Technology [(B.Tech.) includes all Courses listed in Annexure II (1) (b)]
B.Tech. (Agricultural Engineering) [B.Tech. (Agri. Engg.)]
B.Tech. (Food Technology) [B.Tech. (Food Tech)]
B.Tech. (Dairy Technology)

## 1.3.2  Architecture Course :
Bachelor of Architecture (B.Arch.)
## 1.3.3 Medical Courses:
Bachelor of Medicine and Bachelor of Surgery (MBBS)
Bachelor of Dental Surgery (BDS)
Bachelor of Ayurvedic Medicine and Surgery (BAMS)
Bachelor of Siddha Medicine and Surgery (BSMS)
Bachelor of Homoeopathic Medicine and Surgery (BHMS)
Bachelor of Unani Medicine and Surgery (BUMS)

## 12                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

1.3.4 Agriculture,  Forestry,  B.Sc.(Hons)  Co-operation  &  Banking/  B.Sc  (Hons)  Agri
Business  Management,  Climate  Change  &  Environmental  Science,  B.Tech
## Biotechnology Courses:
Bachelor of Science-Agriculture [BSc.(Hons.) Agri.]
Bachelor of Science-Forestry [BSc.(Hons.) Forestry]
Bachelor of Science-[BSc.(Hons.)] B.Sc.(Hons) Co-operation & Banking /B.Sc (Hons)
## Agri Business Management
Bachelor of Science - [BSc. (Hons.] Climate Change & Environmental Science
Bachelor of Technology - B.Tech. Biotechnology

## 1.3.5    Veterinary Course:
Bachelor of Veterinary Science & Animal Husbandry (BVSc. & AH)
## 1.3.6 Fisheries Course:
Bachelor of  Fisheries Science (BFSc.)
## 1.3.7 Pharmacy Course:
Bachelor of Pharmacy (B.Pharm)
1.4 a) Admission to Engineering courses shall be regulated on the basis of merit as assessed by
giving  equal  weightage  of  50:50  to  the  normalized  score  obtained  in  the  Entrance
Examination  for  Engineering  and  the  grade/marks  obtained  in  the  final  year  of  the
qualifying  examination  for  Mathematics,  Physics  and  Chemistry  put  together  in  the
ratio 5:3:2, after effecting the normalization procedure as described in Clause 9.7.4(b),
for  computing  the  Index  mark  out  of  600.  In  case,  the  candidate  has  not  studied
Chemistry, the marks obtained in Computer Science shall be considered. In case, the
candidate  has  not  studied  Chemistry  and  Computer  Science,  the  marks  obtained  in
Biotechnology shall be considered. In case, the candidate has not studied Chemistry,
Computer  Science  and  Biotechnology,  the  marks  obtained  in  Biology  shall  be
considered.  The  marks  as  shown  in  the  mark  list  obtained  from  the  Board  of
Examination of respective Higher Secondary Board shall be considered for academic
eligibility. (As per G.O (Rt) No.1615/2025/HEDN Dated: 26.12.2025)
b)  For  admission  to  the  Architecture  course*,  the  merit  as  assessed  by  giving  equal
weightage  to  the  marks  obtained  in  the  ‘National  Aptitude  Test  in  Architecture’
[NATA], conducted by the Council of Architecture (CoA), and the grade/marks in the
qualifying  examination  will be  the criterion.  [*As per directives of the Council of
## Architecture, India.]
c)  Admission to Medical courses, Agriculture, B.Sc.(Hons) Co-operation & Banking/B.Sc
(Hons)  Agri    Business  Management,  Climate  Change  &  Environmental  Science,
B.Tech  Biotechnology  (Under  Kerala  Agricultural  University),  Forestry,  Veterinary
and Fisheries courses are regulated on the basis of merit as assessed in the National
Eligibility  cum  Entrance  Test  (NEET-UG  2026)  conducted  by  the  National  Testing
Agency (NTA).

## 13                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

d)  Admission to the B.Pharm course is regulated on the basis of marks obtained in the
Kerala Pharmacy Entrance Examination and the rank list prepared based on this as in
clause 9.7.4(f).
1.5    The  Rank  lists  shall  include  all  candidates  qualified  in  the  respective  Entrance
Examinations  conducted  by  the  Commissioner  for  Entrance  Examinations,  Kerala/
National  Testing  Agency  (NTA)/Council  of  Architecture  (CoA)  irrespective  of  their
academic eligibility and category (For admission purposes refer clauses 6.2, 9.7.11(c),
11.4.6 and 11.7.2).
1.6   This  Prospectus  is  subject  to  modification/addition/deletion,  as  may  be  deemed
necessary by the Government.
1.7    Allotment of seats from the Rank Lists for all courses in Self-financing/Autonomous
colleges will be made in accordance with the orders of the Hon’ble Supreme Court of
India/ Hon’ble High Court of Kerala or orders of the Govt. of Kerala/Govt. of India/ as
per the law in existence at the time of Centralised Allotment Process (CAP) and will be
notified separately.
## 2.  COURSES, INSTITUTIONS AND SEATS
2.1      Categorization of Seats in Government and Aided Institutions:
2.1.1  Government  Seats:  Merit  seats  against  which  the  Commissioner  for        Entrance
Examinations makes allotment are called ‘Government Seats’.
(a)  Government seats are available in all the Govt. and Aided Colleges.
(b)  The  availability  of  Government  seats  in  Self-financing  Colleges  run  by
institutions under Govt. control and Private Self-financing colleges/Autonomous
Colleges will be notified separately. Those candidates who seek admission in
Private Self-financing colleges are bound to accept the conditions stipulated in
the  agreement  between  Government,  Self-financing  and  Autonomous  College
## Management(s).
2.1.2  Management Seats: The seats set apart in the Aided institutions, to be filled up by the
Managements  concerned  are  called  Management  Seats.  However,  in  the  case  of
courses  for  which  common  counselling  is  mandated  by  the  respective  Central
Regulatory  Bodies,  the  Management  seats  will  be  included  in  the  Centralized
Allotment Process conducted by the Commissioner for Entrance Examinations.
2.2  Categorization of Seats in Self-Financing/Autonomous Institutions:
The categorization of seats in Self-financing Colleges run by institutions under Govt.
Control, Govt. Cost Sharing Colleges and other Private Self-financing/ Autonomous
colleges will be notified separately. As per the orders of the Hon’ble Supreme Court of
India  dated:  09.05.2017  on  WP(C)  No.  267/2017,  the  allotments/admissions  to  the
State Quota seats in all the Government as well as Private Self Financing Medical and
Dental colleges shall be done through a Common Counselling to be conducted by the
Commissioner  for  Entrance  Examinations.  The  Common  Counselling  will  include
NRI  seats  in  Self  Financing  Medical  &  Dental  Colleges  and  Minority  Community

## 14                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

Quota  seats  in  Private  Self  Financing  Medical  &  Dental  Colleges  having  Minority
Status.  As  per  NCISM  directives,  the  allotment  to  the  state  quota  seats  (including
Management/NRI/Minority  seats,  if  any)  in  Private  Self  Financing  Ayurveda/
Siddha/Unani colleges shall be done through a common counselling, to be conducted
by the Commissioner for Entrance Examinations.
The  All  India  Merit  seats  in  Private  Self  Financing  Medical/  Dental/  Ayurveda/
Siddha/Unani  colleges  are  also  included  in  the  Centralized  Allotment  Process
conducted by the Commissioner for Entrance Examinations.
Note:Autonomous  Colleges  are  the  colleges,  affiliated  to  the  University  conferred  with
Autonomous  status  by  the  University  Grants  Commission  and  notified  as  such  by
University.  The  academics  and  examination  Regulations  applicable  to  Autonomous
Colleges  shall  be  governed  by  the  regulations  /Orders  /Circulars  issued  by  the
University  from  time  to  time,  as  applicable  to  Autonomous  Colleges  Candidates
applied  for  admission  in  Autonomous  Engineering  Colleges  shall  verify  those
regulations and satisfy themselves before applying for it.
## 2.3    Engineering Courses:
2.3.1    The  B.Tech.  Degree  courses  affiliated  to  various  Universities  in  Kerala  including
Autonomous Colleges, under the semester scheme of studies comprise eight semesters.
2.3.2   The B.Tech. (Agricultural Engineering) and the B.Tech. (Food Technology) courses
under the Kerala Agricultural University [KAU].
2.3.3  The  B.Tech.  (Dairy  Technology)  and  B.Tech  (Food  Technology)  courses  under  the
Kerala Veterinary and Animal Sciences University [KVASU].
2.3.4   The B.Tech. (Food Technology) course under the Kerala University of Fisheries and
Ocean Studies [KUFOS].
2.3.5  The  list  of  Engineering  Colleges  and  the  courses  offered  are  given  in Annexure
II (1)(a), VII(1), VII(2). The lists are tentative and not complete.  The final list will be
published  by  the  CEE,  prior  to  the  commencement  of  the  Centralised  Allotment
Process 2026 (CAP-2026).
2.4     Architecture Course: B.Arch. Degree course extends over 10 semesters including one
semester for practical training and one semester for thesis work. (Refer to Annexure II
(1)(a) for the institutions offering the B.Arch. Course). The list  is tentative and  not
complete.  The  final  list  will  be  published  prior  to  the  commencement  of  the CAP-
## 2026.
## 2.5 Medical & Medical Allied Courses:
2.5.1   The Medical courses include MBBS, BDS, BAMS, BSMS, BHMS & BUMS under the
Kerala University of Health Sciences.
2.5.2  The  list  of  institutions  in  which  Medical  courses  are  offered,  the  number  of  seats
available, etc. are given in Annexure III (1), IV (1), V (1), VI (1) & VI (2). The list is
tentative and not complete. The final list will be published prior to the commencement
of CAP-2026.

## 4.            RESERVATION OF SEATS FOR VARIOUS COURSES
4.1     Types of Reservation in Government/ Aided/ KAU/ KVASU/ KUFOS Colleges:
Out  of the total seats available for the various courses, seats will be reserved for
different categories as given under Clauses 4.1.1 to 4.1.5.
4.1.1(i)    Reservation   for   All   India   Quota   for  MBBS/ BDS/ BAMS/ BHMS
Courses  in Govt. Medical/Dental/Ayurveda/Homoeo Colleges:

Fifteen percent of the total sanctioned seats in MBBS/BDS/BAMS/BHMS Courses in
Govt. Medical/Dental/Ayurveda/Homoeo Colleges in the State are set apart for the
allotment  of  the  candidates  by  the  Director  General  of  Health  Services/AACCC,
Government  of  India  on  the  basis  of  the  rank  obtained  in  the  NEET-UG  2026
conducted by the National Testing Agency (NTA), New Delhi. See clause 4.1.11(a)
(ii) Reservation  for  All  India  Quota  for MBBS/BAMS/BSMS/BUMS   Courses  in
Self-   Financing  Medical/Ayurveda/Siddha/Unani colleges:-
Fifteen percent of the seats for the admission of students to   MBBS/ BAMS/ BSMS/
BUMS  Courses  in  Self-Financing  Medical/  Ayurveda/  Siddha/  Unani  Colleges  in
Kerala are set apart for the allotment of candidates irrespective of their Domicile as
per the rank list prepared by the Commissioner for the Entrance Examinations on the
basis of the rank  obtained in the NEET-UG 2026 conducted by the National Testing
Agency (NTA)  New Delhi.  See clause 4.1.11(a) and 4.1.13(a) & (b)
4.1.2  Reservation for Nominees:  These  are  the  seats  set  apart  for  the  nominees  of  the
Government of India, Union Territories or other States for the various courses. [For
details, refer Clauses 4.1.11 (b), 4.1.12, 4.1.13, 4.1.14, 4.1.15]
4.1.3   Reservation for Persons with Disabilities: Leaving the seats set apart under Clauses
4.1.1, 4.1.2 above, all types of supernumerary seats sanctioned, five percent of the
seats  available  for  the  state  for  allotment  from  the  Entrance  rank  lists  for  all  the
courses in all the Government Colleges, Aided colleges and Government Cost-sharing
Engineering  Colleges  are  reserved  for  the  candidates  with  Benchmark  disabilities.
[For details, refer Clause 5.3]
4.1.4  Special Reservation: These are the seats reserved for certain specific categories, for
different courses. [For details, refer Clause 5.2]
4.1.5   Mandatory  Reservation:  Leaving  the  seats  set  apart  for  All  India  Quota,
Government of India Nominees, Special reservations, Persons with Disabilities, all
types  of  supernumerary  seats  sanctioned      and  Management  Quota,  the  remaining
Government  seats  for  each  course  in  Govt./Aided/KAU/KVASU/KUFOS  Colleges

## 17                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

will be distributed as per the mandatory reservation principle as contemplated in G.O.
(P) No.208/66/Edn. Dated 2.5.1966, G.O.(Ms)No.95/08/SCSTDD Dated 06.10.2008,
GO(Ms)  No.  10/2014/BCDD  Dated  23.05.2014,  G.O.  (Ms)  No.128/2020/HEdn.
Dated 20.03.2020 and as modified from time to time.
The percentage break-up of seats as per mandatory reservation is as follows:
(A)       State Merit (SM)  50%
## (B)
Economically  Weaker  Sections  in    General  Category
## (EWS)
## 10%
(C)       Socially and Educationally Backward Classes (SEBC)  30%
a.  Ezhava (EZ)  9%
b.  Muslim (MU)  8%
c.  Other Backward Hindu (BH)  3%
d.  Latin Catholic and Anglo Indian (LA)  3%
e.  Dheevara and related communities (DV)  2%
f.   Viswakarma and related communities (VK)  2%
g.  Kusavan and related communities (KN)  1%
h.  Other Backward Christian (BX)  1%
i.   Kudumbi (KU)  1%
(D)       Scheduled Castes & Scheduled Tribes  10%
a.  Scheduled Castes (SC) 8%
b.  Scheduled Tribes (ST) 2%
## Note
- As per GO(Ms) No. 46/2015/SCSTDD dated: 23.06.2015, the reservation pattern in
Govt.  Medical  College,  Palakkad  (Institute  of  Integrated  Medical  Sciences,
Palakkad) will be as follows:
Scheduled Caste - 70%, Scheduled Tribe - 2%, General Merit – 13% and All
## India Quota- 15%.
-  As per GO (Rt.)No. 1621/2017/H&FWD dated 08.06.2017, the reservation pattern
in Government Medical College, Kollam will be as follows:
State Quota-50%, Wards of Insured Persons under Employees State Insurance
Corporation-35% (Not allotted by CEE), All India Quota-15%.
4.1.6    The total number of seats available for the different courses will be published prior
to the commencement of CAP-2026.
4.1.7    Admission to all the Government seats except the seats reserved for All India Quota
for MBBS/BDS/BAMS/BHMS Courses and Nominees will be made on the basis of
respective rank lists/inter-se merit as may be applicable.

Government and Aided Colleges will be finalised before CAP-2026.

4.1.9  Reservation of seats for Engineering Courses  [B.Tech.]:  The  number  of  seats

Government  of  India  Nominees  and  Special  reservation  categories  is  given  in
Annexure II (2)(a).
4.1.11   Reservation of seats for MBBS & BDS Courses
a) Reservation of seats under All India Quota: Details of seats in Government
Medical/Dental Colleges are given in Annexure III (2).  Details of seats in Self-
Financing Medical colleges will be notified separately.
b) Reservation of seats for Nominees:
(i) Nominees of the Government of India: The Government of India, subject to
the eligibility conditions in clause 6, will make nominations to these seats.
The distribution of seats under this category and other details in respect of
MBBS/BDS courses are available in Annexure III (2).
(ii) Nominees from Union Territory of Andaman & Nicobar Islands: These
seats  are  reserved  for  the  candidates  of  Kerala  origin  settled  in  the  Union
Territory of Andaman and Nicobar Islands. Nominations to these seats will be
made by the Administration of that Union Territory and the candidates must
possess  the  requisite  qualifications  as  provided  under  Clause  6.  The
distribution of seats is given in Annexure III (2).
(iii) Nominees  from  Lakshadweep:  Seats  are  reserved  for  the  candidates  of
Kerala origin settled in Lakshadweep. The candidates should be sponsored by
the  Administration  of  that  Union  Territory  and  must  possess  the  requisite
qualifications as per Clause 6. The distribution of seats is given in Annexure
## III (2).
(iv) Nominee from Jammu & Kashmir: One seat for MBBS will be reserved in
a  Govt.  Medical  College  (by  rotation  every  year  in  the  order  TVM,  ALP,
KTM,  TCM,  KKM,  MLP  ,CMC,  KLM,  PKM,  KNM,  IDM,  PTM)  for  a
nominee from Jammu & Kashmir. Candidate to this seat should be sponsored
by  the  Government  of  Jammu  and  Kashmir  through  the  Higher  Education
Secretary  of  the State.  This  year, the seat  will  be reserved  in  Government
Medical College, Ernakulam. [See Annexure III(2)].

Admission to the seats under 4.1.11(b)(i) to 4.1.11(b)(iv) above should be
completed by the admitting authority concerned and the Director of Medical
Education  will  inform  the  CEE,  through  Government  of  Kerala,  the  un-
availed  seats  in  these  categories  before  the  Third  Round  allotment
conducted  by the CEE. Such seats will be reverted to the mandatory quota.

4.1.12  Reservation  of  seats  for  BHMS  Course:  The  number  of  seats  reserved  under
nominees  and  special  reservation  categories  are  given  in Annexure IV (2).  The

## 19                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

vacant seats, if any, existing in nominee quota,  after the second phase allotment,

4.1.15 Reservation  of  seats  for  B.Pharm  course:  The  number  of  seats  reserved  for
Government  of  India  nominee  and  Special  Reservation  categories  in  B.Pharm
Course is given in Annexure VI(3)(a).
4.2  Types of reservation in Self Financing Colleges: The reservation of seats in Self-
financing Colleges run by institutions under Govt. control and Private Self-financing
colleges will be notified separately.
4.3   Reservation of Seats for Economically Weaker Sections in General category: As
per  the G.O.(MS)No.128/2020/HEDN dated.20.03.2020, Government  have  decided
to  implement  reservation  for  Economically  Weaker  Sections  in  general  category
(EWS) to all Higher Educational Institutions other than Minority Institutions, where
reservation to other backward classes are provided.
## 5.     CLAIMS FOR RESERVATION AND CERTIFICATES TO BE UPLOADED
Note: (i) Claims for Special/Mandatory reservations must be made by a candidate in
the online application and the supporting documents shall be uploaded to the online
application within the stipulated time. The claim has to be specified in the application
in the appropriate places. Claims made after the submission of online application
will not be entertained even if supporting evidences are produced. The claims for
Special and Mandatory reservation once made in the application cannot be altered by
the candidate under any circumstance.
(ii) Only candidates belonging to ‘Keralite’ category as defined in Clause 6.1(i), are
eligible  for  claiming  Special/Mandatory  reservation  in  Government/Aided/Self
Financing  Colleges,  unless  otherwise  specified  in  the  prospectus.  Details  of
reservation of seats, if any, in Self-financing colleges will be notified separately.
5.1   Reservation  for Nominees:  The  categories  of  candidates  who  are  entitled  to  the
Central  Government  reserved  seats  for  admission  to  MBBS/BDS  courses,  and  the
authorities  to  whom  applications  are  to  be  sent,  are  given  in Annexure  III (3).
Categories  of  candidates  who  are  entitled  for  reservation  under  nominees  for
Government BHMS & BAMS courses are available in  Annexure IV (2), V (2) and
Self-Financing  BAMS/BSMS/BUMS  courses  are  available  in Annexure VI(2)(a).
Categories of candidates who are entitled for reservation under nominees for B.Pharm
Course are available in Annexure VI (3)(b).
5.2     Claim for Special Reservation:
(i)  Selection  under  special  reservation  categories  for  admission  to  MBBS,  BDS,
BAMS,BHMS, Agriculture, Forestry, B.Sc.(Hons) Co-operation & Banking/B.Sc
(Hons) Agri  Business Management,Veterinary & Fisheries courses
In the case of special reservation seats earmarked for MBBS, BDS, BAMS, BHMS,
Agriculture,  Forestry,  B.Sc.(Hons)  Co-operation  &  Banking/B.Sc  (Hons)  Agri
Business Management, Veterinary & Fisheries courses, which are filled on the basis
of the Kerala State Rank List of NEET-UG 2026 prepared by the CEE, only those

## 21                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

candidates  satisfying  the  eligibility  conditions  as  per  Clauses  6  and  9.7.5(ii)  &
9.7.5(iii) will be considered.
In the case of candidates whose admissions are governed by inter-se merit list, only
those  candidates  who  figure  in  the  Kerala  State  Rank  List  of  NEET-UG  2026
prepared  by  CEE  as  stipulated  in  pre-para  will  be  considered  while  preparing  the
inter-se  merit  list  for  admission  to  MBBS,  BDS,  BAMS,  BHMS,  Agriculture,
Forestry, Co-operation & Banking,Veterinary & Fisheries courses.
(ii)     All the candidates seeking admission under the ‘Special Reservation Categories’ will
have  to  appear  for  the  Entrance  Examination  concerned  and  find  place  in  the
respective rank list. In case the admissions are based on inter-se merit lists, only those
candidates who have been included in the respective rank lists will be considered for
preparing the inter-se merit list.
(iii)   Candidates should mention the item of reservation claimed in the relevant columns in
the application and should be otherwise eligible as per Clause 6.
(iv)  Candidates should upload required certificates in the prescribed format to the online
application within the stipulated time, as mentioned for each item, in support of the
claim from Clauses 5.2.1 to 5.2.15.
(v)   Selection to the seats mentioned from Clause 5.2.1 to 5.2.14 will be made on the basis
of rank in the respective rank list. Selection to the seats mentioned from 5.2.15 to
5.2.17  (except  5.2.15(iii)),  will  be  made  on  the  basis  of  the  inter-se  merit  of  the
candidates  in  the  merit  list  prepared  for  the  purpose.  For  special  reservations
mentioned from Clause5.2.15 to 5.2.17 (except 5.2.15(iii)), only those candidates who
are included in the respective rank list will be considered for inclusion in the inter-se
merit list.
(vi)   In  cases  where  candidates  are  to  be  allotted  to  the  ‘Special  Reservation’  seats  of
Engineering/  Architecture/  B.Pharm/  Medical/  Agriculture/  Veterinary/  Fisheries
courses on the basis of inter-se merit list, the authorities concerned will forward the
preliminary merit list of candidates prepared on the basis of the proficiency of the
candidate  in  the  respective  fields to  the Commissioner for Entrance  Examinations.
Such preliminary proficiency list should reach the Office of the Commissioner for
Entrance Examinations on or before  30
th
April 2026. Lists received after this date will
not  be  entertained  under  any  circumstance  and  such  seats  will  be  merged  to  the
Mandatory reservation quota.
(vii)     Seats  under  Special  Reservation  in  Self-financing  colleges,  if  available,  will  be
notified  separately.  Such  seats,  if  any,  will  not  be  shifted  to  Government/Aided
colleges under any circumstance. The details of Special Reservation seats earmarked
in Govt./Aided Colleges are given in Annexure II (2) (a), III (2), IV (2), V (2), VI
(3)(a) and VII (4).
5.2.1  Ex-servicemen Quota (XS): Applicants to this category should invariably upload to
the online application, a certificate in Annexure XIII (a)(i)  or (a)(ii) as applicable
obtained not earlier than six months from the last date of application from the Zilla
Sainik Welfare Officer concerned to the effect that he/she is the son/daughter of ex-

## 22                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

serviceman or an ex-serviceman himself/herself. The certificate should clearly show
that  the  benefit  of  reservation  has  not  been  granted  earlier  to  any  member  in  the
family. In the absence of the certificate, the claim will not be considered.
5.2.2     Dependent of Defence Personnel  Killed/Missing/Disabled  in  action  (DK):  This
benefit will be available to one person only from the family concerned in respect of
each  defence  person  killed  in  action/missing  in  action/disabled  either  during  war
hostilities or in peace time circumstances of which are identical to activities during
operational engagements. They should invariably upload a certificate in Annexure
XIII(a)(iii) to the online application obtained not earlier than six months from the
last date of application from the Zilla Sainik Welfare Officer concerned to the effect
that he/she is the son/daughter/widow of the defence person who was killed in action
or  missing  in  action  or  disabled  in  action.  In  the  case  of  disabled  personnel,  the
certificate  should  specify  that  the  concerned  person  was/is  in  receipt  of  disability
pension. The certificate should clearly show that the benefit of reservation has not
been granted earlier to any member in the family. In the absence of the certificate, the
claim will not be considered.
If no suitable candidate under DK category is available for the concession, as per the
existing  order/rules,  the  seats  reserved  for  them  will  be  given  to  the
son/daughter/widow of the defence personnel who died in harness (HR), if they are
otherwise eligible as per Clause 6. They should upload a certificate in Annexure XIII
(a) (iv) to the online application obtained not earlier than six months from the last
date of application from the concerned Zilla Sainik Welfare Officer where the Ex-
servicemen/Widow  is  registered,  to  the  effect  that  the  defence  personnel  had  died
while in service. The certificate should clearly show that the benefit of reservation has
not been granted earlier to any member in the family. In the absence of the certificate,
the claim will not be considered.
If there are still no suitable candidates under HR category, the seats reserved for the
children/widow of defence personnel killed in action/missing in action/disabled will
be  given  to  children  of  Serving  Defence  personnel  or  in  their  absence  to  ex-
servicemen/ children of ex-servicemen.
Only one candidate from a family will be eligible for Special Reservation
quota under Clauses 5.2.1 & 5.2.2.

5.2.3      Serving Defence Personnel (SD): Seats are reserved for sons/daughters of serving
defence personnel from Kerala for admission to Engineering/Architecture/ Medical/
Agricultural/ Veterinary Courses.  Candidates seeking reservation under this category
should upload a certificate in Annexure XIII (b) (i) to the online application obtained
not  earlier  than  six  months  from  the  last  date  of  application  from  the  Officer
Commanding/Local  Military  Authority  to  the  effect  that  the  candidate  is  the
son/daughter of serving defence personnel, with details of the station where he/she
works at present. Certificate obtained for other purposes will not be considered.

## 23                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

If  there  are  no  suitable  candidates  under  SD  category,  the  seat  reserved  for  SD
category will be given to Ex-servicemen (XS) category and in their absence, the seats
will be merged with mandatory quota.
5.2.4    CAPF (RP):  Seats  are reserved for sons/daughters of personnel serving in Central
Armed   Police   Force/Dependent   of   Armed   Police   Force   Personnel
Killed/Missed/Disabled in Action. The Central Armed Police Force (CAPF) include
the organizations such as Assam Rifles (AR), Border Security Force (BSF), Central
Reserved  Police  Force  (CRPF),  Central  Industrial  Security  Force  (CISF),  Indo-
Tibetan Border Police (ITBP), National Security Guard (NSG), Sashastra Seema Bal
(SSB). Candidates seeking admission under this category should upload a certificate
in  Annexure  XIII  (b)(ii)  to  the  online  application  obtained  from  the  Officer
Commanding under whom they are serving/were serving to that effect. The certificate
should have been obtained not earlier than six months from the last date of online
application. The  purpose  of  issue  should  be  shown  clearly  and  the  certificate
issued for other purposes are not acceptable in any case.
Note:- Seats will be reserved for the candidates eligible for reservation under XS, DK, SD,
RP,  PI & PT and  CC categories as defined in Clauses 5.2.1 to  5.2.4, 5.2.16 &
5.2.17    in  Private  Self  Financing  Engineering/  Architecture  Colleges  as  listed  in
Annexure II (2) (b).
5.2.5    Jewish (JW) Quota (For MBBS/BDS courses): One seat each will be reserved for
Jewish community for admission to MBBS and BDS. In case candidates from the
community  are not  available,  the  seat  will  merge with  the  mandatory  reservation
quota. The selection will be on the basis of the Kerala State Rank List of NEET-UG
2026  prepared  by  the  CEE.  The  candidate  claiming  reservation  under  the  Jewish
community quota should upload a certificate from the Village Officer/Tahsildar to
the online application to the effect that he/she belongs to Jewish community (Refer
Annexure III (2)).
5.2.6    Degree holders in MBBS, BHMS (OA) (For BAMS course): One seat in BAMS
course  will  be  reserved  for  the  candidates  having  MBBS  Degree/BHMS  Degree
recognised by any of the Universities in Kerala, subject to the eligibility conditions
under clause 6. Admission to the course is based on the Kerala State Rank List of
NEET-UG 2026 prepared by the CEE. The candidates should upload to the online
application MBBS degree/BHMS degree certificate, as the case may be, to prove
eligibility. Internship certificate and registration certificate should also be uploaded
in support of the claim to the online application. [Refer Annexure V(2)]
5.2.7  Degree holders in Ayush Courses (DA)  (For  MBBS  course):  Eleven  seats  are
reserved for Degree holders in  Ayush courses (Ayurveda, Homoeopathy, Siddha,
Unani) recognized by any of the Universities in Kerala for MBBS course subject to
the  eligibility  conditions  as  per  Clause  6 GO  (Rt)  No.653/2025/H&FWD
Dated:05.03.2025. Admission will be given to Degree holders on the basis of the
Kerala State Rank List of NEET-UG 2026 prepared by the CEE. Candidates should

## 24                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

upload  (a)  Degree  certificate,  (b)  Internship  certificate,  and  (c)  Registration
certificate, in support of the claim to the online application. [Refer Annexure III (2)]
5.2.8  Degree holders in BDS (DM) (For MBBS course):
One seat in the MBBS course is reserved for holders of BDS on rotation basis in one
of the colleges in the order of TVM, KLM, PTM, ALP, KTM, IDM, CMC, TCM,
MLP, KKM, KNM  vide G.O (Ms) No. 101/2023/H&FwD Dated: 28.04.2023 for
the candidates having BDS degree recognised by   any one of the Universities in
Kerala,  subjected  to  the  eligibility  conditions  under  clause  6.    Admission  to  the
course is based on the Kerala State Rank List of NEET UG 2026 prepared by the
CEE.    The  Candidates  should  upload  to  the  online  application  BDS  degree
certificates  to  prove  eligibility.    Internship  certificate  &  registration  certificate
should  also  be  uploaded  in  support  of  the  claim  to  the  online  application  (refer
Annexure  III  (2)).    This  year  the  seat  will  be  reserved  in  Government  Medical
College Alappuzha (ALP) (Refer Annexure III (2))
Note: The candidates applying for the quota of seats specified under Clauses 5.2.6, 5.2.7
&  5.2.8  should  complete  their  internship  before  the  last  date  of  submission  of
KEAM-2026 online applications.
5.2.9   Degree  Holders  in  MBBS/BAMS/BVSc  &  AH/  BSc  (Hons)  Agri/  BFSc/
BSc(Hons) Forestry (OH) (For BHMS Course): One seat in BHMS Course will
be  reserved  for  the  candidates  having  MBBS/BAMS/BVSc.&  AH/BSc.(Hon.)
Agri./BFSc./BSc.(Hon.) Forestry Degree recognised by any of the Universities  in
Kerala.  Admission  will  be  given  on  the  basis  of  the  Kerala  State  Rank  List  of
NEET-UG  2026 prepared by  the  CEE  and  subject to  the eligibility  conditions in
Clause 6. Candidates should upload to the online application the Degree certificate
and if the degree has been taken from outside the State, an eligibility/equivalency
certificate  ofthe  degree  from  any  of  the  Universities  in  Kerala,  should  also  be
uploaded to the online application (Refer Annexure IV (2).As per the Govt.Order
168/2023/AYUSH,  dated:  20.05.2023,  the  seats  for  OH  &  NH  categories  are
interchangeable on rotation basis from the year 2023. This year the seat reserved for
OH category will be in Govt. Homoeo Medical College, Thiruvananthapuram and
NH Category will be in Govt. Homoeo Medical College, Kozhikode.
5.2.10(i) Nurse-Allopathy (NQ): One seat under this quota for MBBS course is reserved for
Nurses (Allopathy) in regular service under Government of Kerala who has  secured
highest  rank  in  NEET  UG  conducted  by  National    Testing  Agency  (GO
(Rt)No.652/2025/H&FWD Dated:05.03.2025). Candidates should upload a Service
Certificate in Annexure XIV (a) from the Head of Office, stating that the candidate
is a Regular Employee in the State Government Service and a registration certificate
issued  by  the  Kerala  Nurses  &  Midwives  Council  to  the  online  application.
Admission will be given on the basis of the Kerala State Rank List of NEET-UG
2026 prepared by the CEE and subject to the eligibility conditions in Clause 6. The
candidates who have undergone Nursing Course outside the State should obtain the

## 25                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

Registration  Certificate  issued  by  the  Nursing  Council  of  respective  States  and
upload to the online application (Refer Annexure III (2).
(ii)  Nurse/Pharmacist-Homoeopathy (NH): In the case of BHMS course one seat is
reserved for Nurses/Pharmacist (Homoeo) and such candidate should have passed
the  Higher  Secondary  or  equivalent  examination  in  addition  to  the  Government
recognised course in Nursing/ Pharmacy (Homoeo). Admission will be given on the
basis  of  the  Kerala  State  Rank  List  of  NEET-UG  2026  prepared  by  the  CEE.
Candidate should upload a service certificate in Annexure XIV (b) from the Head of
the Office in Kerala stating that he/she is a regular employee in Government service
working as Nurse/Pharmacist (Homoeo) to the online application (Refer Annexure
IV (2)).  As per the Govt.Order 168/2023/AYUSH, dated:20.05.2023 the seats for
OH & NH categories are interchangeable on rotation basis from the year 2023.This

Thiruvananthapuram and NH Category will be in Govt. Homoeo Medical College,
## Kozhikode.
(iii) Nurse-Ayurveda (NY): In the case of BAMS course one seat is reserved for Nurses

Rank  List  of  NEET-UG  2026  prepared  by  the  CEE.  Candidate  should  upload  a

stating that he/she is a regular employee in Government service working as Nurse
(Ayurveda), to the online application (Refer Annexure V (2).
5.2.11  Children  of  Agriculturists  for  BSc.(Hons.)  Agri.  and  BVSc.  &  AH  Courses
(CA/CE/CS): An agriculturist should be a person whose main source of income is
derived from the agricultural  sources  including agricultural  labour. The parent  or
guardian of the student shall not be an assessee of Income Tax. The non-agricultural
income of the parents or guardian should not be more than Rs.12000/- per annum.
The Agricultural income and non-agricultural income of the parent/guardian of the
applicant should specifically be mentioned in the income certificate issued by the
competent  authority  not  below  the  rank  of  Village  Officer  of  the  Revenue
Department in the prescribed format in Annexure XVI (a) to be uploaded to the
online  application  for  KEAM-2026  (Refer Annexure  VII  (4).  Eleven  Seats  are
reserved for Open quota (CA), and three seats each are reserved for SC/ST (CS) and
SEBC (CE) under this category. If no suitable candidate is available in SC/ST or
SEBC, the vacant seats will be filled from the Open quota (CA) and if there is still
no  suitable  candidate  in  the  Open  quota  (CA)  the  seats  will  be  merged  with  the
mandatory quota.
5.2.12  Children of Farm Labourers/Permanent Labourers of KAU for BSc. (Hons.)
Agri.,  B.Sc.  (Hons)  Co-operation  &  Banking/  B.Sc  (Hons)  Agri    Business
Management, B.Sc (Hons) Forestry, B.Tech Agri. Engg Courses (LG), BVSc &
AH course under KVASU (LV), BFSc course under KUFOS (LF):  The seats

## 26                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

under the quota in BSc. (Hons.) Agri., B.Sc. (Hons) Co-operation & Banking/ B.Sc
(Hons) Agri  Business Management, and B.Sc (Hons) Forestry, B.Tech Agri. Engg
Courses are reserved for Children of Farm Labourers/Permanent Labourers of KAU.
The seats under the quota in BVSc & AH course is reserved for Children of Farm
Labourers  of  KVASU.  The  seats  under the  quota  in  BFSc  course  is  reserved for
Children of Farm Labourers of KUFOS. Candidates seeking reservation under the
quota  for  children  of  farm  labourers/Permanent  labourers  of  Kerala  Agricultural

Fisheries and Ocean Studies should upload to the online application a certificate in

5.2.13  Children  of  Fishermen  for  BFSc.Course,  B.Tech  Food  Technology  Course
under KUFOS (CF):  Fishermen  are  those  whose  profession  is  fishing  and  their
main  source  of  income  is  from  fishing.  Candidates  seeking  admission  under  the
quota for children of Fishermen should be son/daughter/dependent of a Fisherman.
There are 24 seats reserved for BFSc.Course & 8 seats reserved for B.Tech Food
Technology Course under this quota. The applicant under this quota should upload
a certificate in the prescribed format in Annexure XVI(b) from the Village Officer
concerned stating that he/she is son/daughter/dependent of the Fisherman and stating
that  the  annual  family  income  of  the  applicant  is  not  more  than  Rs.6  lakhs  for
KEAM-2026.  Dependants  are  the  son/daughter/brother/sister  of  Fishermen.
Candidates seeking admission under this quota will be eligible for fee concession,
only if they upload  the certificate  in  the prescribed  format  in Annexure XXXIV
from  Fisheries  Officer  of  Kerala  Fishermen  Welfare  Fund  Board  concerned  (see
clause 12.1.3 and Annexure VII (4).
Note:-Certificate received after the prescribed time limit will not be entertained.
5.2.14  Scouts and Guides for Engineering Courses (SG):  Two  seats  are  reserved  for
Rashtrapathi  Scouts  and  Guides  for  Engineering  Courses.  Candidates  seeking
reservation under this quota should upload the Rashtrapathi Guide Certificate signed
by the President of India to the online application. In the absence of this Certificate,
Specimen Certificate signed by the Director of General Education (DGE), Kerala
and the State Secretary, Kerala State Bharat Scouts and Guides, will be considered
(see Annexure II(2) (a).

Diploma  holders  in  Agricultural  Science  (DG)/  Diploma  in  Organic  Agriculture

the rank list for the Medical & Medical Allied courses prepared by the CEE on the

reserved  for  Diploma  Holders  in  Agricultural  Science  (DG)/  Diploma  in  Organic

## 28                     KEAM 2026© CEE,TVM

A selection committee constituted by the respective Universities will assign marks
to the candidates under Agricultural Assistants (AG) referred in Clause 5.2.15 (i)
and the categories referred in 5.2.15 (ii) out of 500, considering the academic merit
(Higher Secondary = 200) higher qualification (BSc. = 100, MSc. = 100) and length
of service (100). The list of candidates under the respective categories along with the
marks allotted to them as above will be prepared and sent to the Commissioner for
Entrance Examinations to reach him on or before 30
th
## April, 2026.
The marks out of 500, awarded to the candidates for academic merit will be added to
the  marks  obtained  by  the  respective  candidates  in  the  respective  Entrance
Examinations (provided they are ranked in the  concerned Entrance Examination),
computed out of 500  so that the candidates would be eligible for a maximum of
1000 marks.  The merit list for each of the above category would be prepared on the
basis of inter-se merit of the candidate as computed above.
(iii) Diploma  holders  in  Laboratory  Techniques,  Feed  Technology,  Poultry
Production Programmes, BSc Degree holders in Poultry Production & Business
Management  (DP)  conducted    by  KVASU    and  VHSE  (Livestock
Management),  HSE  (Dairy  Farmer  Entrepreneur  course,  Small  Poultry
Farmer course) (LK) for BVSc & AH course: Candidates who claim  the seats
reserved for Diploma holders in Laboratory Techniques, Feed Technology, Poultry
Production  Programmes,  Degree  holders  in  BSc  Poultry  Production  &  Business
Management  (DP),  conducted  by  KVASU    and  VHSE  (Livestock  Management),
HSE (Dairy Farmer Entrepreneur course, Small Poultry Farmer course) holders (LK)
shall upload the Diploma certificate in Laboratory Techniques, Feed Technology,
Poultry  Production  Programmes,  degree  certificate  in  BSc.  PPBM  and  VHSE
(Livestock Management), HSE (Dairy Farmer Entrepreneur course, Small Poultry
Farmer course)  certificates to the online application. Final year VHSE (Livestock
Management)/  HSE  (Dairy  Farmer  Entrepreneur  course,  Small  Poultry  Farmer
course), students   can also claim the seats reserved for BVSc. & AH course and
such  candidates  should  upload  the  respective  course  certificate  to  the  online
application.  Such  candidates  shall  produce  their  pass  certificate  on  the  date  of
admission.  The  allotment  to  the  seats  reserved  for  Laboratory  Techniques,  Feed
Technology, Poultry Production Programmes, BSc Poultry Production & Business
Management  conducted  by  KVASU  and  VHSE  (Livestock  Management)/HSE
(Dairy Farmer Entrepreneur course, Small Poultry Farmer course) shall be based on
the rank list for the Medical & Medical Allied courses prepared by the CEE on the
basis of NEET-UG 2026 rank list. To claim the seats for Laboratory Techniques,
Feed  Technology,    Poultry  Production  Programmes,  BSc  Poultry  Production  &
Business Management conducted by KVASU and VHSE (Livestock Management)/
HSE  (Dairy  Farmer  Entrepreneur  course,  Small  Poultry  Farmer  course)  the
candidates must take the NEET-UG 2026 and the NEET SCORE to be submitted in
the website as and when notified by the CEE.
